  ;!function() {
    var traceidComponents = {}

    //购物流程 traceid 追踪
    gbExposeTraceid = function(type, payload) {
          try {
              var traceids = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('saTraceids'))

              if(!traceids) {
                  traceids = {}
              }
              var defaultTraceid = 'spc`' + Date.now() + '`'+ (window.gbGetCookie('cookieId') || '')
              var traceid =''
              if(type == 'setComponent') {
                  if(!traceidComponents[payload.componentName]) {
                      traceid = payload.traceid || defaultTraceid
                      if(payload.params){
                          traceid +='`'+payload.params
                      }
                      traceidComponents[payload.componentName] = traceid
                  }else{
                      traceid = traceidComponents[payload.componentName]
                  }
              } else if(type == 'getComponent') {
                  if(!traceidComponents[payload.componentName]){
                      traceidComponents[payload.componentName] = defaultTraceid
                  }
                  traceid = traceidComponents[payload.componentName]
              } else if(type == 'setProduct') {
                  traceid = payload.traceid || defaultTraceid
                  if(payload.params){
                      traceid +='`'+payload.params
                  }
                  traceids[payload.goods_id] = traceid
              } else if(type == 'getProduct') {
                  if(!traceids[payload.goods_id]){
                    traceids[payload.goods_id] = defaultTraceid
                  }
                  traceid = traceids[payload.goods_id]
              }
              sessionStorage.setItem('saTraceids', JSON.stringify(traceids))
              return traceid
          } catch (error) {
              console.log(error);
          }
      }
  }();

  <script>
   // SensorPageInfo.pageNm 在其他地方会重新赋值
    var SensorPageInfo = {
        pageNm: ''
    }
    function getServerUrl() {
        var environment = 'production';
        var url = '';
        switch(environment) {
            case 'gray':
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=project_gray'
                break
            case 'production':
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=production'
                break
            default:
                url = 'https://api-sensors.shein.com/sa?project=default'
                break
        }
        return url
    }
    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = "; " + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
        if (parts.length >= 2) {
            return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
        } else {
            return undefined;
        }
    }
    function getShowLog() {
        // sensor-analysisi-show-log  2 展示 3 隐藏 
        // 0 根据环境变量判断
        var tag = 0
        var result = 0
        try {
            tag = sessionStorage.getItem('sensor-analysisi-show-log') || getCookie('sensor-show-log') || 0
        } catch(e) {}
        switch (Number(tag)) {
            case 2:
                result = true
                break
            case 3:
                result = false
                break
            case 0:
                // result = 'production' === 'production' ? false : true
                resule = false
                break
        }
        return result
    }

  function GB_ga_getCookie(name){
    var value = "; " + document.cookie;
    var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
    if (parts.length >= 2) {
      return decodeURIComponent(parts.pop().split(";").shift())
    } else {
      return ''
    }
  }
  function dateFormat(fmt, d) {
    const o = {
      'M+': d.getMonth() + 1, // 月份
      'd+': d.getDate(), // 日
      'h+': d.getHours(), // 小时
      'm+': d.getMinutes(), // 分
      's+': d.getSeconds(), // 秒
      'q+': Math.floor((d.getMonth() + 3) / 3), // 季度
      S: d.getMilliseconds() // 毫秒
    }
    if (/(y+)/.test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (d.getFullYear() + '').substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length))
    for (var k in o) if (new RegExp('(' + k + ')').test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, RegExp.$1.length == 1 ? o[k] : ('00' + o[k]).substr(('' + o[k]).length))
    return fmt
  }

    //get url query params

    if (r != null) return unescape(r[2]); return null;
  }

  }

    var S_Module = S_Module || {};
        (function(){
            var modules = {};
            //定义
            S_Module.define = function(name, obj){
                modules[name] = obj;
            };
            //引用模块
            S_Module.require = function(name){
                if( modules[name] )
                return modules[name];
                // else
                // console.error('模块 ' + name + ' 加载失败');
            };
            S_Module.initModule = function(arr, opts){
                opts = opts || {};
                for( var i=0; i<arr.length; i++ ){
                    var name = arr[i];
                    var module = modules[name];
                    if( module ){
                        module.initialize && module.initialize(opts);
                    } else {
                        // console.error('模块 ' + name + ' 加载失败');
                    }
                }
            };
        })();

    <script>
     ;(function() {
    var setCookie = function(name, val, expires, domain) {
        /*setCookie start*/
        var __CurrentMainDomain__ = (function() {
            var hostnameArray = location.hostname.split('.')
            return '.' + hostnameArray.slice(-2).join('.')
        })()

        //domain = domain || __CurrentMainDomain__;
        var text = String(encodeURIComponent(val))
        var date = new Date()
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + Number(expires) * 1000)
        text += '; expires=' + date.toUTCString()
        // domain
        text += '; path=/'
        if (typeof domain != 'undefined' && domain != '') {
            text += '; domain=' + __CurrentMainDomain__
        }

        document.cookie = name + '=' + text
    }
    setCookie('cate_channel_type', 2, 3600 * 24 * 30)
    
})();
    </script>

                        throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object');
                    }

                            for (var key in source) {
                                if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, key)) {
                                    target[key] = source[key];
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    return target;
                };

   <script data-id="index-stylegallery-vue" type="text/javascript">
    Vue.component('index-stylegallery', {
	    template: '#index-stylegallery',
	    data: function() {
	    	return {
	    		goods: {},
          navData: [],
	    		status: { loading: -1, loginModal: false},
	    		quickOpenEvent: { status: { open: false } },
          language: "us",
          loginModal: {type: '', ref: null},
          forgetPassword: { showForm: false, },
          gaCache: {},
          added_wish: {},
          index: 0
	    	}
	    },
	    computed: {
        },
        watch: {
        },
        mounted: function() {
            this.bindEvent();
			if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
				GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
			}
        },
	    methods: {
	    	bindEvent: function() {
                var self = this;
                $( function(){
                    self.loadGoodsData();
                    self.getNavData();
                    }
                )

                $(window).scroll(function(e){
                    if(self.scrollTimeout){
                        clearTimeout(self.scrollTimeout);
                    }
                    self.scrollTimeout = setTimeout(self.sa_scrollHandler,500);
                });
	    	},
	    	loadGoodsData: function() {
                var self = this;
	    		$.ajax({
                    url: '//api-shein.shein.com/social_wear/wear_list_pc?ps=10&callback=?',
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    data: {
                        language: gbCalcSocialWearLang(),
                        siteUid: typeof gbCommonInfo !== 'undefined' && gbCommonInfo.SiteUID,
                    },
                    headers: {
                        SocialSiteFrom: 'pc'
                    },
                    success: function(data) {
                        if(data && data.info && data.info.wear_img_list && data.info.wear_img_list.length) {
                            self.goods = data.info.wear_img_list;
                            self.nextTick();
                            $('.outfit-container').css('visibility', 'visible');
                            $(window).scroll();
                        } else {
                            $('.outfit-container').hide();
                        }
                    }
			    });
	    	},
	    	// opt
            quickViewOpen: function(opt) {
              var self = this;
              this.index = opt.index
            	if(this.status.loading >= 0) return;
            	this.status.loading = opt.index;
                this.sa_clickPhoto(opt.goodsId,opt.index+1);
                
                window.QuickViewInstance.show({
                    goodsId: opt.goodsId,
                    config: {
                        styleGellery: {
                            _oimg: opt.oimg || '',
                            _simg: opt.simg || ''
                        }
                    },
                    callback: {
                        handleOpenQuickViewDone: function() {
                            // self.quickOpenEvent.status.open = false
                            self.status.loading = -1;
                        },
                        handleOpenLogin: self.openLoginModal,
                        handleAddWishDone: self.qvAddWishSuc
                    },
                    analysis: {
                        index: opt.index,
                        sa: {
                            code: 'styleGallery',
                            activity_from: 'style_gallery'
                        },
                        ga: {
                            eventCategory: '推荐列表',
                            moduleName: 'recommend',
                            moduleTitle: 'StyleGallery'
                        }
                    }
                })

                /**
                 *
                this.quickOpenEvent = {
                    status: {
                        open: true,
                        pageType: 'home'
                    },
                    data: {
                        goodsId: opt.goodsId,
                        styleGalleryData: {
                            _oimg: opt.oimg || '',
                            _simg: opt.simg || '',
                            pageType: 'styleGallery-home'
                        },
                        index: opt.index,
                        activity_from: 'style_gallery',
                        code: 'styleGallery',
                        eventCategory: '推荐列表',
                        moduleName: 'recommend',
                        gaTitle: 'StyleGallery'
                    },
                    callback: function(data, code) {
                        self.quickOpenEvent.status.open = false
                        // self.quickOpenEvent = { status: { open: false } };
                    	self.status.loading = -1;
                    }
                }
                *  
                * */
            },
            qvAddWishSuc: function(goods_id) {
              if(this.added_wish[goods_id]) {
                this.$set(this.added_wish, goods_id, 0)
              } else {
                this.$set(this.added_wish, goods_id, 1)
              }
            },
            //DOM渲染完成后数据处理函数
            nextTick: function() {
            	var self = this;
            	var _prevButton = '.j-outfit-prev';
	            var _nextButton = '.j-outfit-next';

	            this.$nextTick(function () {
	            	self.outfitSwiper = new Swiper ('.j-outfit-swiper', {
		                direction: 'horizontal',
		                prevButton: _prevButton,
		                nextButton: _nextButton,
		                spaceBetween: 20,
		                slidesPerView: 5,
		                slidesPerGroup : 5,
		                lazyLoadingInPrevNext : true,
		                lazyLoading: true,
                        onSlideChangeEnd: function(swiper){
                            self.sa_exposePhotos();
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('slideChangeEnd', {swiper: swiper})
                            }
							if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
			                    GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
			                }
                        },
                        onSlidePrevEnd: function(swiper){
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('SlidePrevEnd')
                            }
                        },
                        onSlideNextEnd: function(swiper){
                            if(typeof(gaEventCenter) != 'undefined') {
                                gaEventCenter.$emit('SlideNextEnd')
                            }
                        }
		            });
					if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
						GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
					}
		        });
            },
            getNavData: function(times) {
                var self = this, navLoadFailTime = 0;
                if(times) navLoadFailTime = times;
                var navAjax = $.ajax({
                    url: '//api-shein.shein.com/social_wear/label_list_pc',
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    timeout: 5000,
                    data: {
                        language: gbCalcSocialWearLang(),
                        label_type:1,
                        siteUid: typeof gbCommonInfo !== 'undefined' && gbCommonInfo.SiteUID,
                    },
                    headers: {
                        SocialSiteFrom: 'pc'
                    }
                })
                .done(function(data) {
                    if(data && data.code == 0 && data.info && data.info.category_list && data.info.category_list.length) {

                        self.navData = data.info.category_list;
                        self.$nextTick(function() {
                            new Swiper ('.j-tags-swiper', {
                                direction: 'horizontal',
                                prevButton: '.j-tags-prev',
                                nextButton: '.j-tags-next',
                                spaceBetween: 15,
                                slidesPerView: 'auto',
                                slidesPerGroup : 5,
                                onSlideChangeEnd: function(){
                                    self.sa_exposeMenu();
									if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
					                    GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
					                }
                                }
                            });
							if (typeof GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance != 'undefined') {
								GB_SHEIN_lazyLoadInstance.update()
							}
                        })
                        $(window).scroll();
                    }
                })
                .fail(function() {
                    navLoadFailTime++;
                    if(navLoadFailTime < 5) {
                        self.getNavData(navLoadFailTime);
                    }
                })
            },
            clickNav: function(opt) {
                if(opt.url) {
                    window.location.href = opt.url;
                    this.sa_clickMenu(opt.labelId,opt.pitPos);
                }
            },
			// 登录弹框
			openLoginModal: function(addToWish) {
				this.status.loginModal = true;
				this.loginModal.type = 'qv-add-wish';
                this.loginModal.ref = addToWish;
                SHEIN_LOGIN.show({ cb: this.loginModalSucCb, from: 'wishlist' })
			},
			loginModalSucCb: function() {
				this.status.loginModal = false;
				SHEIN_W.userModule.update_top_login();
				cart_module.reload();
				if (this.loginModal.type === 'qv-add-wish') {
                    // this.loginModal.ref.addToWish();
                    typeof this.loginModal.ref == 'function' && this.loginModal.ref()
                    
				}
			},
            loginModalClose: function() {
                this.status.loginModal = false
            },
            transformImg: transformImg,
            sa_scrollHandler:function(){
                //style gallery 曝光
                var stylegalleryMenu = $('.c-style-gallery-nav');
                if(!stylegalleryMenu.hasClass("sa_expose")){
                    if($(window).height() >= stylegalleryMenu.get(0).getBoundingClientRect().bottom * 0.8){
                        this.sa_exposeMenu();
                        this.sa_exposePhotos();
                        stylegalleryMenu.addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                }
            },
            sa_exposeMenu:function(){
                var stylegalleryMenu = $('.c-style-gallery-nav');
                var clientRect = stylegalleryMenu.get(0).getBoundingClientRect();
                var param = '';
                var self = this;
                stylegalleryMenu.find('.swiper-slide').each(function(index,item){
                    var itemClientRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
                    if(itemClientRect.left>=clientRect.left-20 && itemClientRect.right<=clientRect.right+20 && !$(item).hasClass('sa_expose')){
                        param += (index+1)+'`'+self.navData[index].label_id+',';
                        $(item).addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                });
                if(param.length>0){
                    param = param.substring(0,param.length-1);
                    sa('send',{'activity_name':'expose_home_style_gallery_style','activity_param':{
                        content_list:param
                    }});
                }
            },
            sa_exposePhotos:function(){
                var stylegalleryPhotos = $('.c-style-gallery-nav').prev();
                var clientRect = stylegalleryPhotos.get(0).getBoundingClientRect();
                var param = '';
                var self = this;
                stylegalleryPhotos.find('.swiper-slide').each(function(index,item){
                    var itemClientRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
                    if(itemClientRect.left>=clientRect.left-20 && itemClientRect.right<=clientRect.right+20 && !$(item).hasClass('sa_expose')){
                        param += (index+1)+'`'+self.goods[index].goods_id+',';
                        $(item).addClass('sa_expose');
                    }
                });
                if(param.length>0){
                    param = param.substring(0,param.length-1);
                    sa('send',{'activity_name':'expose_home_style_gallery_goods','activity_param':{
                        goods_list:param,
                    }});
                }
            },
            sa_clickPhoto:function(_goodId,_pitPos){
                sa('send',{'activity_name':'click_home_style_gallery_goods','activity_param':{
                    goods_list:_pitPos+'`'+_goodId,
                }});
            },
            sa_clickMenu:function(_labelId,_pitPos){
                if(typeof _labelId == 'undefined'){
                    _labelId = 0;
                    _pitPos = 1;
                }
                sa('send',{'activity_name':'click_home_style_gallery_style','activity_param':{content_list:_pitPos+'`'+_labelId}});
            }
	    }
	});
